I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
bug: [GC] WasmEdge segfault on `ref.cast eqref` after `table.get`
### Summary

# WasmEdge SIGSEGV: `ref.cast` on null reference from concrete-typed table

## Version

- WasmEdge 0.16.1, commit `3ad922d67525975f6b4ec0e382604d91f97354bd`
- Linux 5.15.0-168-generic x86\_64

## Minimal Reproducer

```wat
(module
  (type $s (struct))
  (table 1 (ref null $s))
  (func (export "run")
    i32.const 0
    table.get 0      ;; null (ref null $s) from uninitialized slot
    ref.cast eqref   ;; CRASH
    drop
  )
)
```

```bash
wasm-tools parse crash.wat -o crash.wasm
wasm-tools validate crash.wasm   # OK
wasmedge crash.wasm run          # Segmentation fault
d8 run.js -- crash.wasm                 # OK
```

## GDB Analysis

```bash
gdb -batch -ex "run" -ex "bt" -ex "x/5i \$rip-4" -ex "info registers rax r15" \
  -ex "x/2gx \$r15" --args /users/khan22/.wasmedge/bin/wasmedge crash.wasm run
```

```
Thread 2 "wasmedge" received signal SIGSEGV, Segmentation fault.
0x00007ffff1c6ca05 in ?? () from /users/khan22/.wasmedge/lib/libwasmedge.so.0.1.0

   0x7ffff1c6ca08:  mov    %rdi,%rcx

   0x7ffff1c6ca11:  je     0x7ffff1c6ca28

r15  0x7fffec000cd0

0x7fffec000cd0:  0x0000000800630000   0x0000000000000000

```

Corresponding location in `/users/khan22/.wasmedge/lib/libwasmedge.so.0.1.0` (text base `0x7ffff141c000`):

```bash
objdump -d --start-address=0x8509a0 --stop-address=0x850a30 \
  /users/khan22/.wasmedge/lib/libwasmedge.so.0.1.0
```

```asm
850a01:  49 8b 47 08          mov    0x8(%r15),%rax
850a05:  48 8b 00             mov    (%rax),%rax       ; NULL deref
850a0e:  48 85 c0             test   %rax,%rax         ; null check after deref maybe?
850a11:  74 15                je     850a28
```

## (Potential) Root Cause

`table.get` on a concrete-typed table (`(table N (ref null $type))`) returns a null reference with object pointer `0x0` on the interpreter value stack. The `ref.cast` handler then dereferences this pointer to read the type descriptor before checking for null. The null check exists but is placed after the dereference.

## Acknowledgement
This bug has been found during development process of `GCsmith`.

   361	  // Copy the value type here due to handling the externalized case.
   362	  auto VT = Ref.getType();
   363	  if (VT.isExternalized()) {
   364	    VT = ValType(TypeCode::Ref, TypeCode::ExternRef);
   365	  }
   366	  const auto *ModInst = StackMgr.getModule();
   367	  assuming(ModInst);
   368	  Span<const AST::SubType *const> GotTypeList = ModInst->getTypeList();
   369	  if (!VT.isAbsHeapType()) {
   370	    auto *Inst = Ref.getPtr<Runtime::Instance::CompositeBase>();
   371	    // Reference must not be nullptr here because the null references are typed
   372	    // with the least abstract heap type.
   373	    if (Inst->getModule()) {
   374	      GotTypeList = Inst->getModule()->getTypeList();
   375	    }
   376	  }
   377	
   378	  if (AST::TypeMatcher::matchType(ModInst->getTypeList(), VTTest, GotTypeList,
   379	                                  VT)) {

   382	    return static_cast<uint32_t>(0);

   398	    auto *Inst = Ref.getPtr<Runtime::Instance::CompositeBase>();
   399	    // Reference must not be nullptr here because the null references are typed

   306	Expect<void> Executor::runArrayInitElemOp(
   307	    Runtime::StackManager &StackMgr, const uint32_t Cnt, const uint32_t TypeIdx,
   308	    const uint32_t ElemIdx, const AST::Instruction &Instr) const noexcept {

   312	  EXPECTED_TRY(
   313	      arrayInitElem(StackMgr, Ref, TypeIdx, ElemIdx, DstIdx, SrcIdx, Cnt)
   314	          .map_error([&](auto E) {

   317	                E, Instr, [&]() { return logArrayOOB(E, DstIdx, Cnt, Ref); },
   318	                [&]() { return logTableOOB(E, *ElemInst, SrcIdx, Cnt); });

   322	
   323	Expect<void>
   324	Executor::runRefTestOp(const Runtime::Instance::ModuleInstance *ModInst,
   325	                       ValVariant &Val, const AST::Instruction &Instr,
   326	                       const bool IsCast) const noexcept {
   327	  // Copy the value type here due to handling the externalized case.
   328	  auto VT = Val.get<RefVariant>().getType();
   329	  if (VT.isExternalized()) {
   330	    VT = ValType(VT.isNullableRefType() ? TypeCode::RefNull : TypeCode::Ref,
   331	                 TypeCode::ExternRef);
   332	  }
   333	  Span<const AST::SubType *const> GotTypeList = ModInst->getTypeList();
   334	  if (!VT.isAbsHeapType()) {
   335	    auto *Inst =
   336	        Val.get<RefVariant>().getPtr<Runtime::Instance::CompositeBase>();
   337	    // Reference must not be nullptr here because the null references are typed
   338	    // with the least abstract heap type.
   339	    if (Inst->getModule()) {
   340	      GotTypeList = Inst->getModule()->getTypeList();
   341	    }
   342	  }
   343	
   344	  if (AST::TypeMatcher::matchType(ModInst->getTypeList(), Instr.getValType(),
   345	                                  GotTypeList, VT)) {
   346	    if (!IsCast) {
   347	      Val.emplace<uint32_t>(1U);
   348	    }
   349	  } else {
   350	    if (IsCast) {
   351	      spdlog::error(ErrCode::Value::CastFailed);
   352	      spdlog::error(ErrInfo::InfoMismatch(Instr.getValType(), VT));
   353	      spdlog::error(
   354	          ErrInfo::InfoInstruction(Instr.getOpCode(), Instr.getOffset()));
   355	      return Unexpect(ErrCode::Value::CastFailed);
   356	    } else {
   357	      Val.emplace<uint32_t>(0U);
   358	    }
   359	  }
   360	  return {};
   361	}

   334	  bool isValType() const noexcept {
   335	    return Inner.Data.TypeFlag == TypeEnum::ValType;
   336	  }
   337	  ValType getValType() const noexcept { return Inner.Type; }
   338	  uint32_t getTypeIndex() const noexcept { return Inner.Data.Idx; }
   339	
   340	private:
   341	  // The ValType has reserved the padding 2 bytes.
   342	  // Therefore, use the first byte to store the flag.
   343	  union {
   344	    // The ValType has 8 bytes length.
   345	    ValType Type;
   346	    // The Data struct has 8 bytes length.
   347	    struct {
   348	      TypeEnum TypeFlag;
   349	      uint8_t Paddings[3];
   350	      uint32_t Idx;
   351	    } Data;
   352	  } Inner;
   353	};
   354	
   355	// <<<<<<<< Type definitions <<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<
   356	
   357	// >>>>>>>> Value definitions >>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>>
   358	
   359	/// FuncRef definition.
   360	namespace Runtime::Instance {
   361	class FunctionInstance;
   362	class StructInstance;
   363	class ArrayInstance;
   364	} // namespace Runtime::Instance
   365	
   366	/// RefType variant definition.
   367	struct RefVariant {
   368	  // Constructors.
   369	  RefVariant() noexcept { setData<void>(TypeCode::ExternRef); }
   370	  RefVariant(const ValType &VT) noexcept { setData<void>(VT); }
   371	  RefVariant(const ValType &VT, const RefVariant &Val) noexcept {
   372	    setData(VT, Val.getPtr<void>());
   373	  }
   374	
   375	  template <typename T> RefVariant(const T *P) noexcept {
   376	    setData(TypeCode::ExternRef, reinterpret_cast<const void *>(P));
   377	  }
   378	  template <typename T> RefVariant(const ValType &VT, const T *P) noexcept {
   379	    setData(VT, reinterpret_cast<const void *>(P));
   380	  }
   381	  RefVariant(const Runtime::Instance::FunctionInstance *P) noexcept {
   382	    setData(TypeCode::FuncRef, reinterpret_cast<const void *>(P));
   383	  }
   384	  RefVariant(const Runtime::Instance::StructInstance *P) noexcept {
   385	    setData(TypeCode::StructRef, reinterpret_cast<const void *>(P));
   386	  }
   387	  RefVariant(const Runtime::Instance::ArrayInstance *P) noexcept {
   388	    setData(TypeCode::ArrayRef, reinterpret_cast<const void *>(P));
   389	  }
   390	
   391	  // Getter of type.
   392	  const ValType &getType() const noexcept {
   393	    return reinterpret_cast<const ValType &>(toArray()[0]);
   394	  }
   395	  ValType &getType() noexcept {
   396	    return reinterpret_cast<ValType &>(toArray()[0]);
   397	  }
   398	
   399	  // Getter of pointer.
   400	  template <typename T> T *getPtr() const noexcept {
   401	    return reinterpret_cast<T *>(toArray()[1]);
   402	  }
   403	
   404	  // Check is null.
   405	  bool isNull() const { return getPtr<void>() == nullptr; }
   406	
   407	  // Getter of the raw data.
   408	  uint64x2_t getRawData() const noexcept { return Data; }
   409	
   410	private:
   411	  // Helper function of converting data to array.
   412	  const std::array<uint64_t, 2> &toArray() const noexcept {
   413	    return reinterpret_cast<const std::array<uint64_t, 2> &>(Data);
   414	  }
   415	  std::array<uint64_t, 2> &toArray() noexcept {
   416	    return reinterpret_cast<std::array<uint64_t, 2> &>(Data);
   417	  }
   418	
   419	  // Helper function to set the content.
   420	  template <typename T>
   421	  void setData(const ValType &VT, const T *Ptr = nullptr) noexcept {
   422	    getType() = VT;
   423	    toArray()[1] = reinterpret_cast<uintptr_t>(Ptr);
   424	  }
   425	
   426	  // Member data.
   427	  uint64x2_t Data;
   428	};
   429	
   430	/// ValVariant for all value types.
   431	using ValVariant =
   432	    Variant<uint32_t, int32_t, uint64_t, int64_t, float, double, uint128_t,
   433	            int128_t, uint64x2_t, int64x2_t, uint32x4_t, int32x4_t, uint16x8_t,
   434	            int16x8_t, uint8x16_t, int8x16_t, floatx4_t, doublex2_t,
   435	            RefVariant>;

   457	  }

    85	class ValType {
    86	public:
    87	  // Note: The padding bytes are reserved and should not be written.
    88	  ValType() noexcept = default;
    89	  // General constructors for initializing data.
    90	  ValType(TypeCode C, TypeCode HT, uint32_t I) noexcept {
    91	    Inner.Data.Externalize = 0;
    92	    Inner.Data.Code = C;

    97	    std::copy_n(R.cbegin(), 8, Inner.Raw);

    99	  // Constructor for the value type codes without heap type immediates.
   100	  ValType(TypeCode C) noexcept {
   101	    Inner.Data.Externalize = 0;
   102	    Inner.Data.Idx = 0;
   103	    switch (C) {
   104	    case TypeCode::I32:
   105	    case TypeCode::I64:
   106	    case TypeCode::F32:
   107	    case TypeCode::F64:
   108	      // Number type
   109	    case TypeCode::V128:
   110	      // Vector type
   111	    case TypeCode::I8:
   112	    case TypeCode::I16:
   113	      // Packed type
   114	      Inner.Data.Code = C;
   115	      Inner.Data.HTCode = TypeCode::Epsilon;
   116	      break;
   117	    case TypeCode::NullExnRef:
   118	    case TypeCode::NullFuncRef:
   119	    case TypeCode::NullExternRef:
   120	    case TypeCode::NullRef:
   121	    case TypeCode::FuncRef:
   122	    case TypeCode::ExternRef:

   127	    case TypeCode::ArrayRef:

   129	      // Abstract heap type
   130	      Inner.Data.Code = TypeCode::RefNull;
   131	      Inner.Data.HTCode = C;

   380	  }
   381	
   382	  /// Matcher: Match 2 defined types.
   383	  static bool matchType(Span<const SubType *const> ExpTypeList, uint32_t ExpIdx,
   384	                        Span<const SubType *const> GotTypeList,
   385	                        uint32_t GotIdx) noexcept {
   386	    if (ExpIdx >= ExpTypeList.size() || GotIdx >= GotTypeList.size()) {
   387	      return false;
   388	    }
   389	    if (isDefTypeEqual(ExpTypeList, ExpIdx, GotTypeList, GotIdx)) {
   390	      return true;
   391	    }
   392	    const auto *GotType = GotTypeList[GotIdx];
   393	    for (auto TIdx : GotType->getSuperTypeIndices()) {
   394	      if (matchType(ExpTypeList, ExpIdx, GotTypeList, TIdx)) {
   395	        return true;
   396	      }
   397	    }
   398	    return false;
   399	  }
   400	
   401	  /// Matcher: Match 2 value types.
   402	  static bool matchType(Span<const SubType *const> ExpTypeList,
   403	                        const ValType &Exp,
   404	                        Span<const SubType *const> GotTypeList,
   405	                        const ValType &Got) noexcept {
   406	    if (!Exp.isRefType() && !Got.isRefType() &&
   407	        Exp.getCode() == Got.getCode()) {
   408	      // Match for the non-reference type case.
   409	      return true;
   410	    }
   411	    if (Exp.isRefType() && Got.isRefType()) {
   412	      // Nullable matching.
   413	      if (!Exp.isNullableRefType() && Got.isNullableRefType()) {
   414	        return false;
   415	      }
   416	
   417	      // Match heap type.
   418	      if (Exp.isAbsHeapType() && Got.isAbsHeapType()) {
   419	        // Case 1: Both abstract heap type.
   420	        return matchTypeCode(Exp.getHeapTypeCode(), Got.getHeapTypeCode());
   421	      } else if (Exp.isAbsHeapType()) {
   422	        // Case 2: Match a type index to abstract heap type.
   423	        if (Got.getTypeIndex() >= GotTypeList.size()) {
   424	          return false;
   425	        }
   426	        return matchTypeCode(
   427	            Exp.getHeapTypeCode(),
   428	            GotTypeList[Got.getTypeIndex()]->getCompositeType().expand());
   429	      } else if (Got.isAbsHeapType()) {
   430	        // Case 3: Match abstract heap type to a type index.
   431	        if (Exp.getTypeIndex() >= ExpTypeList.size()) {
   432	          return false;
   433	        }
   434	        TypeCode ExpandGotType =
   435	            ExpTypeList[Exp.getTypeIndex()]->getCompositeType().expand();
   436	        switch (Got.getHeapTypeCode()) {
   437	        case TypeCode::NullRef:
   438	          return matchTypeCode(TypeCode::AnyRef, ExpandGotType);
   439	        case TypeCode::NullFuncRef:
   440	          return matchTypeCode(TypeCode::FuncRef, ExpandGotType);
   441	        case TypeCode::NullExternRef:
   442	          return matchTypeCode(TypeCode::ExternRef, ExpandGotType);
   443	        default:
   444	          return false;
   445	        }
   446	      } else {
   447	        // Case 4: Match defined types.
   448	        return matchType(ExpTypeList, Exp.getTypeIndex(), GotTypeList,
   449	                         Got.getTypeIndex());
   450	      }
   451	    }
   452	    return false;
   453	  }
   454	
   455	private:
   456	  /// Matcher: Helper for checking the equivalent of 2 defined types.
   457	  static bool isDefTypeEqual(Span<const SubType *const> LHSList,
   458	                             uint32_t LHSIdx,
   459	                             Span<const SubType *const> RHSList,
   460	                             uint32_t RHSIdx) {

    30	class TableInstance {
    31	public:
    32	  TableInstance() = delete;
    33	  TableInstance(const AST::TableType &TType) noexcept
    34	      : TabType(TType),
    35	        Refs(TType.getLimit().getMin(), RefVariant(TType.getRefType())),
    36	        InitValue(RefVariant(TType.getRefType())) {
    37	    // The reftype should a nullable reference because of no init ref.
    38	    assuming(TType.getRefType().isNullableRefType());
    39	  }
    40	  TableInstance(const AST::TableType &TType, const RefVariant &InitVal) noexcept
    41	      : TabType(TType), Refs(TType.getLimit().getMin(), InitVal),
    42	        InitValue(InitVal) {
    43	    // If the reftype is not a nullable reference, the init ref is required.
    44	    assuming(TType.getRefType().isNullableRefType() || !InitVal.isNull());
    45	  }
    46	
    47	  /// Get size of table.refs
    48	  uint64_t getSize() const noexcept {
    49	    // The table size is binded with the limit in table type.
    50	    return TabType.getLimit().getMin();
    51	  }
    52	
    53	  /// Getter of table type.
    54	  const AST::TableType &getTableType() const noexcept { return TabType; }
    55	
    56	  /// Check is out of bound.
    57	  bool checkAccessBound(const uint64_t Offset,
    58	                        const uint64_t Length) const noexcept {
    59	    // Due to applying the Memory64 proposal, we should avoid the overflow issue
    60	    // of the following code:
    61	    //   return Offset + Length <= Limit;
    62	    const uint64_t Limit = TabType.getLimit().getMin();
    63	    return std::numeric_limits<uint64_t>::max() - Offset >= Length &&
    64	           Offset + Length <= Limit;
    65	  }
    66	
    67	  /// Grow table with initialization value.
    68	  bool growTable(const uint64_t Count, const RefVariant &Val) noexcept {
    69	    if (Count == 0) {
    70	      return true;
    71	    }
    72	    uint64_t MaxSizeCaped = getMaxAddress(TabType.getLimit().getAddrType());
    73	    const uint64_t Min = TabType.getLimit().getMin();
    74	    assuming(MaxSizeCaped >= Min);
    75	    if (TabType.getLimit().hasMax()) {
    76	      const uint64_t Max = TabType.getLimit().getMax();
    77	      MaxSizeCaped = std::min(Max, MaxSizeCaped);
    78	    }
    79	    if (Count > MaxSizeCaped - Min) {
    80	      return false;
    81	    }
    82	    Refs.resize(Refs.size() + Count);
    83	    std::fill_n(Refs.end() - static_cast<std::ptrdiff_t>(Count), Count, Val);
    84	    TabType.getLimit().setMin(Min + Count);
    85	    return true;
    86	  }
    87	  bool growTable(const uint64_t Count) noexcept {
    88	    return growTable(Count, InitValue);
    89	  }
    90	
    91	  /// Get slice of Refs[Offset : Offset + Length - 1]
    92	  Expect<Span<const RefVariant>> getRefs(const uint64_t Offset,
    93	                                         const uint64_t Length) const noexcept {
    94	    // Check the accessing boundary.
    95	    if (!checkAccessBound(Offset, Length)) {
    96	      spdlog::error(ErrCode::Value::TableOutOfBounds);
    97	      spdlog::error(ErrInfo::InfoBoundary(Offset, Length, getSize()));
    98	      return Unexpect(ErrCode::Value::TableOutOfBounds);
    99	    }
   100	    return Span<const RefVariant>(
   101	        Refs.begin() + static_cast<std::ptrdiff_t>(Offset), Length);
   102	  }
   103	
   104	  /// Replace the Refs[Dst :] by Slice[Src : Src + Length)
   105	  Expect<void> setRefs(Span<const RefVariant> Slice, const uint64_t Dst,
   106	                       const uint64_t Src, const uint64_t Length) noexcept {
   107	    // Check the accessing boundary.
   108	    if (!checkAccessBound(Dst, Length)) {
   109	      spdlog::error(ErrCode::Value::TableOutOfBounds);
   110	      spdlog::error(ErrInfo::InfoBoundary(Dst, Length, getSize()));
   111	      return Unexpect(ErrCode::Value::TableOutOfBounds);
   112	    }
   113	
   114	    // Check the input data validation.
   115	    if (std::numeric_limits<uint64_t>::max() - Src < Length ||
   116	        Src + Length > Slice.size()) {
   117	      spdlog::error(ErrCode::Value::TableOutOfBounds);
   118	      spdlog::error(ErrInfo::InfoBoundary(Src, Length, Slice.size()));
   119	      return Unexpect(ErrCode::Value::TableOutOfBounds);
   120	    }

   135	  /// Fill the Refs[Offset : Offset + Length - 1] by Val.
   136	  Expect<void> fillRefs(const RefVariant &Val, const uint64_t Offset,
   137	                        const uint64_t Length) noexcept {
   138	    // Check the accessing boundary.
   139	    if (!checkAccessBound(Offset, Length)) {
   140	      spdlog::error(ErrCode::Value::TableOutOfBounds);
   141	      spdlog::error(ErrInfo::InfoBoundary(Offset, Length, getSize()));
   142	      return Unexpect(ErrCode::Value::TableOutOfBounds);
   143	    }
   144	
   145	    // Fill the references.
   146	    std::fill_n(Refs.begin() + static_cast<std::ptrdiff_t>(Offset), Length,
   147	                Val);
   148	    return {};
   149	  }
   150	
   151	  /// Get the elem address.
   152	  Expect<RefVariant> getRefAddr(const uint64_t Idx) const noexcept {
   153	    if (Idx >= Refs.size()) {
   154	      spdlog::error(ErrCode::Value::TableOutOfBounds);
   155	      spdlog::error(ErrInfo::InfoBoundary(Idx, 1, getSize()));
   156	      return Unexpect(ErrCode::Value::TableOutOfBounds);
   157	    }
   158	    return Refs[Idx];
   159	  }
   160	
   161	  /// Set the elem address.
   162	  Expect<void> setRefAddr(const uint64_t Idx, const RefVariant &Val) {
   163	    if (Idx >= Refs.size()) {
   164	      spdlog::error(ErrCode::Value::TableOutOfBounds);
   165	      spdlog::error(ErrInfo::InfoBoundary(Idx, 1, getSize()));
   166	      return Unexpect(ErrCode::Value::TableOutOfBounds);
   167	    }
   168	    Refs[Idx] = Val;
   169	    return {};
   170	  }
   171	
   172	private:
   173	  /// \name Data of table instance.
   174	  /// @{
   175	  AST::TableType TabType;
   176	  std::vector<RefVariant> Refs;
   177	  RefVariant InitValue;
   178	  /// @}
   179	};
   180	
   181	} // namespace Instance
   182	} // namespace Runtime
   183	} // namespace WasmEdge
   184

   368	  static bool matchTypes(Span<const SubType *const> TypeList,

USAGE
	build/tools/wasmedge/wasmedge [SUBCOMMANDS] [OPTIONS] [--] WASM_OR_SO [ARG ...]

SUBCOMMANDS
	compile
		Wasmedge compiler subcommand
	run
		Wasmedge runtime tool subcommand

OPTIONS
	
-h|--help
		Show this help messages
	
-v|--version
		Show version information
	
--reactor
		Enable reactor mode. Reactor mode calls `_initialize` if exported.
	
--dir
		Binding directories into WASI virtual filesystem. Each directory can be
		specified as --dir `host_path`. You can also map a guest directory to a host
		directory by --dir `guest_path:host_path`, where `guest_path` specifies the
		path that will correspond to `host_path` for calls like `fopen` in the guest.
		The default permission is `readwrite`, however, you can use --dir
		`guest_path:host_path:readonly` to make the mapping directory become a read
		only mode.
	
--env
		Environ variables. Each variable can be specified as --env `NAME=VALUE`.
	
--enable-instruction-count
		Enable generating code for counting Wasm instructions executed.
	
--enable-gas-measuring
		Enable generating code for counting gas burned during execution.
	
--enable-time-measuring
		Enable generating code for counting time during execution.
	
--enable-all-statistics
		Enable generating code for all statistics options include instruction
		counting, gas measuring, and execution time
	
--enable-jit
		Enable Just-In-Time compiler for running WASM
	
--enable-coredump
		Enable coredump when WebAssembly enters a trap
	
--coredump-for-wasmgdb
		Enable coredump for wasm-gdb to debug
	
--force-interpreter
		Forcibly run WASM in interpreter mode.
	
--allow-af-unix
		Enable UNIX domain sockets
	
--wasm-1
		Set as WASM 1.0 standard.
	
--wasm-2
		Set as WASM 2.0 standard.
	
--wasm-3
		Set as WASM 3.0 standard (default).
	
--disable-import-export-mut-globals
		Disable Import/Export of mutable globals proposal
	
--disable-non-trap-float-to-int
		Disable Non-trapping float-to-int conversions proposal
	
--disable-sign-extension-operators
		Disable Sign-extension operators proposal
	
--disable-multi-value
		Disable Multi-value proposal

     9	// Serialize heap type. See "include/loader/serialize.h".
    10	Expect<void>
    11	Serializer::serializeHeapType(const ValType &Type, ASTNodeAttr From,
    12	                              std::vector<uint8_t> &OutVec) const noexcept {
    13	  TypeCode Code = Type.getHeapTypeCode();
    14	  switch (Code) {
    15	  case TypeCode::ExternRef:
    16	    if (unlikely(!Conf.hasProposal(Proposal::ReferenceTypes))) {
    17	      return logNeedProposal(ErrCode::Value::MalformedElemType,
    18	                             Proposal::ReferenceTypes, From);
    19	    }
    20	    [[fallthrough]];
    21	  case TypeCode::FuncRef:
    22	    OutVec.push_back(static_cast<uint8_t>(Code));
    23	    return {};
    24	  case TypeCode::NullFuncRef:
    25	  case TypeCode::NullExternRef:
    26	  case TypeCode::NullRef:
    27	  case TypeCode::AnyRef:
    28	  case TypeCode::EqRef:
    29	  case TypeCode::I31Ref:
    30	  case TypeCode::StructRef:
    31	  case TypeCode::ArrayRef:
    32	    if (!Conf.hasProposal(Proposal::GC)) {
    33	      return logNeedProposal(ErrCode::Value::MalformedRefType, Proposal::GC,
    34	                             From);
    35	    }
    36	    OutVec.push_back(static_cast<uint8_t>(Code));
    37	    return {};
    38	  case TypeCode::TypeIndex:
    39	    if (unlikely(!Conf.hasProposal(Proposal::FunctionReferences))) {
    40	      return logNeedProposal(ErrCode::Value::MalformedRefType,
    41	                             Proposal::FunctionReferences, From);
    42	    }
    43	    serializeS33(static_cast<int64_t>(Type.getTypeIndex()), OutVec);
    44	    return {};
    45	  case TypeCode::NullExnRef:
    46	  case TypeCode::ExnRef:
    47	    if (unlikely(!Conf.hasProposal(Proposal::ExceptionHandling))) {
    48	      return logNeedProposal(ErrCode::Value::MalformedRefType,
    49	                             Proposal::ExceptionHandling, From);
    50	    }
    51	    OutVec.push_back(static_cast<uint8_t>(Code));
    52	    return {};
    53	  default:
    54	    if (likely(Conf.hasProposal(Proposal::ReferenceTypes))) {
    55	      return logSerializeError(ErrCode::Value::MalformedRefType, From);
    56	    } else {
    57	      return logSerializeError(ErrCode::Value::MalformedElemType, From);
    58	    }
    59	  }
    60	}

    62	// Serialize reference type. See "include/loader/serialize.h".
    63	Expect<void>
    64	Serializer::serializeRefType(const ValType &Type, ASTNodeAttr From,
    65	                             std::vector<uint8_t> &OutVec) const noexcept {
    66	  TypeCode Code = Type.getCode();
    67	  switch (Code) {
    68	  case TypeCode::Ref:
    69	    if (unlikely(!Conf.hasProposal(Proposal::FunctionReferences))) {
    70	      return logNeedProposal(ErrCode::Value::MalformedRefType,
    71	                             Proposal::FunctionReferences, From);
    72	    }
    73	    OutVec.push_back(static_cast<uint8_t>(Code));
    74	    return serializeHeapType(Type, From, OutVec);
    75	  case TypeCode::RefNull:
    76	    if (!Type.isAbsHeapType()) {
    77	      OutVec.push_back(static_cast<uint8_t>(Code));
    78	    }
    79	    return serializeHeapType(Type, From, OutVec);
    80	  default:
    81	    if (likely(Conf.hasProposal(Proposal::ReferenceTypes))) {
    82	      return logSerializeError(ErrCode::Value::MalformedRefType, From);
    83	    } else {
    84	      return logSerializeError(ErrCode::Value::MalformedElemType, From);
    85	    }
    86	  }
    87	}

    89	// Serialize value type. See "include/loader/serialize.h".
    90	Expect<void>
    91	Serializer::serializeValType(const ValType &Type, ASTNodeAttr From,
    92	                             std::vector<uint8_t> &OutVec) const noexcept {
    93	  TypeCode Code = Type.getCode();
    94	  switch (Code) {
    95	  case TypeCode::I32:
    96	  case TypeCode::I64:
    97	  case TypeCode::F32:
    98	  case TypeCode::F64:
    99	    OutVec.push_back(static_cast<uint8_t>(Code));
   100	    return {};
   101	  case TypeCode::I8:
   102	  case TypeCode::I16:
   103	    if (!Conf.hasProposal(Proposal::GC)) {
   104	      return logNeedProposal(ErrCode::Value::MalformedValType, Proposal::GC,
   105	                             From);
   106	    }
   107	    OutVec.push_back(static_cast<uint8_t>(Code));
   108	    return {};
   109	  case TypeCode::V128:
   110	    if (unlikely(!Conf.hasProposal(Proposal::SIMD))) {
   111	      return logNeedProposal(ErrCode::Value::MalformedValType, Proposal::SIMD,
   112	                             From);
   113	    }
   114	    OutVec.push_back(static_cast<uint8_t>(Code));
   115	    return {};
   116	  case TypeCode::Ref:
   117	  case TypeCode::RefNull:
   118	    return serializeRefType(Type, From, OutVec);
   119	  default:
   120	    return logSerializeError(ErrCode::Value::MalformedValType, From);
   121	  }
   122	}

   124	// Serialize limit. See "include/loader/serialize.h".
   125	Expect<void>
   126	Serializer::serializeLimit(const AST::Limit &Lim,
   127	                           std::vector<uint8_t> &OutVec) const noexcept {
   128	  // Limit: 0x00 + min:u32
   129	  //       |0x01 + min:u32 + max:u32
   130	  //       |0x02 + min:u32 (shared, invalid)
   131	  //       |0x03 + min:u32 + max:u32 (shared)
   132	  //       |0x04 + min:u64
   133	  //       |0x05 + min:u64 + max:u64
   134	  //       |0x06 + min:u64
   135	  //       |0x07 + min:u64 + max:u64
   136	  //
   137	  // we encode all of them in u64
   138	  uint8_t Flag = 0;
   139	  if (Lim.isShared()) {
   140	    Flag |= 0x02U;
   141	  }
   142	  if (Lim.hasMax()) {
   143	    Flag |= 0x01U;
   144	  }
   145	  if (static_cast<AST::Limit::LimitType>(Flag) >=
   146	      AST::Limit::LimitType::SharedNoMax) {
   147	    if (Conf.hasProposal(Proposal::Threads)) {
   148	      if (unlikely(!Lim.hasMax())) {
   149	        return logSerializeError(ErrCode::Value::SharedMemoryNoMax,
   150	                                 ASTNodeAttr::Type_Limit);
   151	      }
   152	    } else {
   153	      return logSerializeError(ErrCode::Value::IntegerTooLarge,
   154	                               ASTNodeAttr::Type_Limit);
   155	    }
   156	  }
   157	  OutVec.push_back(Flag);
   158	  serializeU64(Lim.getMin(), OutVec);
   159	  if (Lim.hasMax()) {
   160	    serializeU64(Lim.getMax(), OutVec);
   161	  }
   162	  return {};
   163	}
   164

   177	    } else {
   178	      OutVec.push_back(static_cast<uint8_t>(TypeCode::Sub));
   179	    }
   180	    serializeU32(static_cast<uint32_t>(SType.getSuperTypeIndices().size()),

   221	// Serialize function type. See "include/loader/serialize.h".
   222	Expect<void>
   223	Serializer::serializeType(const AST::FunctionType &Type,
   224	                          std::vector<uint8_t> &OutVec) const noexcept {
   225	  // Function type: paramtypes:vec(valtype) + returntypes:vec(valtype).
   226	  // Param types: vec(valtype).
   227	  serializeU32(static_cast<uint32_t>(Type.getParamTypes().size()), OutVec);
   228	  for (auto &VType : Type.getParamTypes()) {
   229	    EXPECTED_TRY(serializeValType(VType, ASTNodeAttr::Type_Function, OutVec));
   230	  }
   231	  // Return types: vec(valtype).
   232	  if (unlikely(!Conf.hasProposal(Proposal::MultiValue)) &&
   233	      Type.getReturnTypes().size() > 1) {
   234	    return logNeedProposal(ErrCode::Value::MalformedValType,
   235	                           Proposal::MultiValue, ASTNodeAttr::Type_Function);
   236	  }
   237	  serializeU32(static_cast<uint32_t>(Type.getReturnTypes().size()), OutVec);
   238	  for (auto &VType : Type.getReturnTypes()) {
   239	    EXPECTED_TRY(serializeValType(VType, ASTNodeAttr::Type_Function, OutVec));
   240	  }
   241	  return {};
   242	}

   252	    spdlog::error(ErrInfo::InfoAST(ASTNodeAttr::Type_Table));
   253	    return E;
   254	  });

b=bytearray()
b += b'\0asm' + bytes([1,0,0,0])
# type
sec=bytes([2, 0x5f,0x00, 0x60,0x00,0x00])
b += bytes([1,len(sec)]) + sec
# function
sec=bytes([1,1])
b += bytes([3,len(sec)]) + sec
# table

   631	  /// Matcher: Helper for matching 2 type codes.
   632	  static bool matchTypeCode(TypeCode Exp, TypeCode Got) noexcept {
   633	    // Handle the equal cases first.
   634	    if (Exp == Got) {
   635	      return true;
   636	    }
   637	
   638	    // Match the func types: nofunc <= func
   639	    if (Exp == TypeCode::FuncRef || Exp == TypeCode::NullFuncRef) {
   640	      return Got == TypeCode::NullFuncRef;
   641	    }
   642	    if (Got == TypeCode::FuncRef || Got == TypeCode::NullFuncRef) {
   643	      return false;
   644	    }
   645	
   646	    // Match the extern types: noextern <= extern
   647	    if (Exp == TypeCode::ExternRef || Exp == TypeCode::NullExternRef) {
   648	      return Got == TypeCode::NullExternRef;
   649	    }
   650	    if (Got == TypeCode::ExternRef || Got == TypeCode::NullExternRef) {
   651	      return false;
   652	    }
   653	
   654	    // Match the exception types: noexn <= exn
   655	    if (Exp == TypeCode::ExnRef || Exp == TypeCode::NullExnRef) {
   656	      return Got == TypeCode::NullExnRef;
   657	    }
   658	    if (Got == TypeCode::ExnRef || Got == TypeCode::NullExnRef) {
   659	      return false;
   660	    }
   661	
   662	    // Match the other types: none <= i31 | struct | array <= eq <= any
   663	    switch (Exp) {
   664	    case TypeCode::I31Ref:
   665	    case TypeCode::StructRef:
   666	    case TypeCode::ArrayRef:
   667	      // This will filter out the i31/struct/array unmatch cases.
   668	      return Got == TypeCode::NullRef;
   669	    case TypeCode::EqRef:
   670	      return Got != TypeCode::AnyRef;
   671	    case TypeCode::AnyRef:
   672	      return true;
   673	    default:
   674	      break;
   675	    }

   461	void Executor::cleanNumericVal(ValVariant &Val,

    93	Expect<void> Executor::runBrTableOp(Runtime::StackManager &StackMgr,
    94	                                    const AST::Instruction &Instr,
    95	                                    AST::InstrView::iterator &PC) noexcept {
    96	  // Get value on top of stack.
    97	  uint32_t Value = StackMgr.pop().get<uint32_t>();
    98	
    99	  // Do branch.
   100	  auto LabelTable = Instr.getLabelList();
   101	  const auto LabelTableSize = static_cast<uint32_t>(LabelTable.size() - 1);
   102	  if (Value < LabelTableSize) {
   103	    return branchToLabel(StackMgr, LabelTable[Value], PC);
   104	  }
   105	  return branchToLabel(StackMgr, LabelTable[LabelTableSize], PC);
   106	}

   108	Expect<void> Executor::runBrOnCastOp(Runtime::StackManager &StackMgr,
   109	                                     const AST::Instruction &Instr,
   110	                                     AST::InstrView::iterator &PC,
   111	                                     bool IsReverse) noexcept {
   112	  // Get value on top of stack.
   113	  const auto *ModInst = StackMgr.getModule();
   114	  const auto &Val = StackMgr.getTop().get<RefVariant>();
   115	  const auto &VT = Val.getType();
   116	  Span<const AST::SubType *const> GotTypeList = ModInst->getTypeList();
   117	  if (!VT.isAbsHeapType()) {
   118	    auto *Inst = Val.getPtr<Runtime::Instance::CompositeBase>();
   119	    // Reference must not be nullptr here because the null references are typed
   120	    // with the least abstract heap type.
   121	    if (Inst->getModule()) {
   122	      GotTypeList = Inst->getModule()->getTypeList();
   123	    }
   124	  }
   125	
   126	  ValType NormalizedVT = VT;
   127	  if (NormalizedVT.isExternalized()) {
   128	    // An externalized reference must appear as an 'externref' to the matcher.
   129	    // We preserve the nullability (Ref vs RefNull).
   130	    NormalizedVT =
   131	        ValType(VT.isNullableRefType() ? TypeCode::RefNull : TypeCode::Ref,
   132	                TypeCode::ExternRef);
   133	  }
   134	
   135	  bool MatchResult = AST::TypeMatcher::matchType(ModInst->getTypeList(),
   136	                                                 Instr.getBrCast().RType2,
   137	                                                 GotTypeList, NormalizedVT);
   138	  if (MatchResult != IsReverse) {
   139	    return branchToLabel(StackMgr, Instr.getBrCast().Jump, PC);
   140	  }
   141	  return {};
   142	}

   149	      spdlog::error(ErrCode::Value::NonNullRequired);
   150	      spdlog::error("    Cannot pass a null reference as argument of {}."sv,
   151	                    ParamTypes[I]);
   152	      return Unexpect(ErrCode::Value::NonNullRequired);
   153	    }
   154	  }
   155	
   156	  Runtime::StackManager StackMgr;
   157	
   158	  // Call runFunction.
   159	  EXPECTED_TRY(runFunction(StackMgr, *FuncInst, Params).map_error([](auto E) {
   160	    if (E != ErrCode::Value::Terminated) {
   161	      dumpStackTrace(Span<const uint32_t>{StackTrace}.first(StackTraceSize));
   162	    }
   163	    return E;
   164	  }));
   165	
   166	  // Get return values.
   167	  std::vector<std::pair<ValVariant, ValType>> Returns(RTypes.size());
   168	  for (uint32_t I = 0; I < RTypes.size(); ++I) {
   169	    auto Val = StackMgr.pop();
   170	    const auto &RType = RTypes[RTypes.size() - I - 1];
   171	    if (RType.isRefType()) {
   172	      // For the reference type cases of the return values, they should be
   173	      // transformed into abstract heap types due to the opaque of type indices.
   174	      auto &RefType = Val.get<RefVariant>().getType();
   175	      if (RefType.isExternalized()) {
   176	        // First handle the forced externalized value type case.
   177	        RefType = ValType(TypeCode::Ref, TypeCode::ExternRef);
   178	      }
   179	      if (!RefType.isAbsHeapType()) {
   180	        // The instance must not be nullptr because the null references are
   181	        // already dynamic typed into the top abstract heap type.
   182	        auto *Inst =
   183	            Val.get<RefVariant>().getPtr<Runtime::Instance::CompositeBase>();
   184	        assuming(Inst);
   185	        // The ModInst may be nullptr only in the independent host function
   186	        // instance. Therefore the module instance here must not be nullptr
   187	        // because the independent host function instance cannot be imported and
   188	        // be referred by instructions.
   189	        const auto *ModInst = Inst->getModule();
   190	        auto *DefType = *ModInst->getType(RefType.getTypeIndex());
   191	        RefType =
   192	            ValType(RefType.getCode(), DefType->getCompositeType().expand());
   193	      }
   194	      // Should use the value type from the reference here due to the dynamic
   195	      // typing rule of the null references.
   196	      Returns[RTypes.size() - I - 1] = std::make_pair(Val, RefType);
   197	    } else {
   198	      // For the number type cases of the return values, the unused bits should
   199	      // be erased due to the security issue.
   200	      cleanNumericVal(Val, RType);
   201	      Returns[RTypes.size() - I - 1] = std::make_pair(Val, RType);
   202	    }
   203	  }
   204	
   205	  // After execution, the value stack size should be 0.
